# 더 월드 41 룩스테라-재료 수급로 참변 수색 원문 로그

**GM:** 지난 날, 유적 의뢰를 마치고 돌아온 일행은 충격적인 소식을 듣게 됩니다.
여러분이 유적을 탐사하고 비밀을 얻고 있을 때 다른 모험가들이 나머지 두개의 의뢰 요청서를
들고 나갔고, 처참한 결과로 이어졌다는 사실.
두 팀 통합 한명을 제외하고는 전부 사망하였으며 의뢰도 실패했습니다. 호송대는 납치되어 소
식이 두절되었고 재료 수급팀은 거대한 짐승을 목격했다고 전해 들었습니다.

**크리스 반데드:** 이 일에 대해 크리스 반데드가 짚히는 점이 있다며 회관에서 정보를 뱉고 있습니다.
한 편, 오늘의 일행이 될 사람들은 뭘 하고 있을까요.

**매그너스:** (그게 왜 진조잘못이더냐?)

네모(Nemo)

**순대:** Illusory Script (Emerald Pen) (Legacy)
You write on parchment, paper, or some other suitable writing material and imbue
it with a potent illusion that lasts for the duration.
To you and any creatures you designate when you cast the spell, the writing
appears normal, written in your hand, and conveys whatever meaning you
intended when you wrote the text. To all others, the writing appears as if it were
written in an unknown or magical script that is unintelligible. Alternatively, you
can cause the writing to appear to be an entirely different message, written in a
different hand and language, though the language must be one you know.
Should the spell be dispelled, the original script and the illusion both disappear.
A creature with truesight can read the hidden message.
(에메랄드 펜으로 가진 정보들을 다 기록합니다 네모만 확인할 수 있는 글입니다

**Rage:** You can imbue yourself with a primal power called Rage, a force that grants you
extraordinary might and resilience. You can enter it as a Bonus Action if you
aren’t wearing Heavy armor.
You can enter your Rage the number of times shown for your Barbarian level in
the Rages column of the Barbarian Features table. You regain one expended use
when you finish a Short Rest, and you regain all expended uses when you finish a
Long Rest.
While active, your Rage follows the rules below.
Damage Resistance. You have Resistance to Bludgeoning, Piercing, and Slashing
damage.
Rage Damage. When you make an attack using Strength—with either a weapon
or an Unarmed Strike—and deal damage to the target, you gain a bonus to the
damage that increases as you gain levels as a Barbarian, as shown in the Rage
Damage column of the Barbarian Features table.
Strength Advantage. You have Advantage on Strength checks and Strength
saving throws.
No Concentration or Spells. You can’t maintain Concentration, and you can’t
cast spells.
Duration. The Rage lasts until the end of your next turn, and it ends early if you
don Heavy armor or have the Incapacitated condition. If your Rage is still active
on your next turn, you can extend the Rage for another round by doing one of
the following:
Make an attack roll against an enemy.
Force an enemy to make a saving throw.
Take a Bonus Action to extend your Rage.
Each time the Rage is extended, it lasts until the end of your next turn. You can
maintain a Rage for up to 10 minutes.

**Dig Deep:** You can use a Bonus Action to dig deep. For 10 minutes, you have Resistance to
Bludgeoning, Piercing, and Slashing damage and you ignore the effects of
Exhaustion levels less than 6.
Once you use this feature, you can’t use it again until you finish a Long Rest
unless you gain 1 Exhaustion level (no action required by you) to restore your
use of it.

When you make your first attack roll on your turn, you can decide to attack
recklessly. Doing so gives you Advantage on attack rolls using Strength until the
start of your next turn, but attack rolls against you have Advantage during that
time.

**Shillelagh:** A Club or Quarterstaff you are holding is imbued with nature’s power. For the
duration, you can use your spellcasting ability instead of Strength for the attack
and damage rolls of melee attacks using that weapon, and the weapon’s
damage die becomes a d8. If the attack deals damage, it can be Force damage
or the weapon’s normal damage type (your choice).
The spell ends early if you cast it again or if you let go of the weapon.
Cantrip Upgrade. The damage die changes when you reach levels 5 (d10), 11
(d12), and 17 (2d6).

**Haste:** Choose a willing creature that you can see within range. Until the spell ends, the
target’s Speed is doubled, it gains a +2 bonus to Armor Class, it has Advantage
on Dexterity saving throws, and it gains an additional action on each of its turns.
That action can be used to take only the Attack (one attack only), Dash,
Disengage, Hide, or Utilize action.
When the spell ends, the target is Incapacitated and has a Speed of 0 until the
end of its next turn, as a wave of lethargy washes over it.

용의 분노 지팡이 [Shillelagh]
이 무기로 공격 굴림에서 20이 나올 때마다, 대상으로부터 5피트 이내에 있는 선택한 각 생
명체는 5의 번개 피해를 입습니다.
행동으로, 무기에서 9미터(30피트) 반경의 파괴적인 에너지 원뿔을 방출할 수 있습니다. 해
당 범위 내의 모든 생명체는 민첩성 내성 굴림(난이도 16)을 해야 하며, 실패 시 8d6의 번개
피해를 입고, 성공 시에는 절반의 피해를 입습니다. 이 행동은 한 번 사용하면 다음 날 새벽까
지 다시 사용할 수 없습니다.
🎲 1d20 + 3 + max(-2,6) + 2 = 18
🎲 1d10 + max(-2,6) + 0 + 2 = 18
🎲 2d6 = 7

**Moxie:** Your experiences of beating the odds have given you a moxie you can channel
in the midst of battle. This swagger is represented by a number of Moxie Points.
Your Pugilist level determines the maximum number of points you have, as
shown in the Moxie Points column of the Pugilist Features table.
You can spend these points to enhance or fuel certain Pugilist features. You start
knowing three such features: Brace Up, One-Two Punch, and Stick and Move,
each of which is detailed below.
When you expend a Moxie Point, it is unavailable until you finish a Short or
Long Rest, at the end of which you regain all your expended points.
Brace Up. You can use a Bonus Action and expend 1 Moxie Point to brace for
attacks. When you do so, roll your Fisticuffs die, and gain a number of
Temporary Hit Points equal to the number rolled plus your Pugilist level and
your Constitution modifier. These Temporary Hit Points vanish if any remain
after 10 minutes.
One-Two Punch. You can expend 1 Moxie Point to make two Unarmed Strikes
as a Bonus Action.
Stick and Move. You can use a Bonus Action and expend 1 Moxie Point to make
an Unarmed Strike and take the Dash or Disengage action.

**Mugfist Knuckles:** These brass knuckles are plated with cheap faux gold that wouldn’t fool even
the most casual observer.
You gain a +1 bonus to attack rolls and damage rolls made with this magic
weapon. When you score a Critical Hit against an enemy with this magic
weapon, you gain GP equal to the creature’s Challenge Rating (or level if it does
not have a Challenge Rating). Creatures with a Challenge Rating less than 1
count as 0.
🎲 1d20 + 5 + 3 + 1 = 18
🎲 1d8 + 5 + 1 = 11

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**이브:** 비알
(쌀먹펀치 ㄷㄷ

**안톤:** 마르도스

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

level above 3.

**Cross Counter:** You can block the brunt of an attack and launch one of your own in the same
fluid motion. When you take damage from a melee attack, you can take a
Reaction and expend 1 Moxie Point to reduce the damage dealt to you by that
attack by 1d10 plus your Strength modifier and Pugilist level.
If you reduce the damage to 0, you can make an Unarmed Strike or attack with
a Pugilist weapon against a creature within your reach as part of the same
Reaction.
🎲 (1d10 + 5) + 5 = 11

**11뎀 감소:** 안톤 gains 2 temp HP

**안톤:** 마르도스
감소뎀이 들어온건가?

**Moxie:** Your experiences of beating the odds have given you a moxie you can channel
in the midst of battle. This swagger is represented by a number of Moxie Points.
Your Pugilist level determines the maximum number of points you have, as
shown in the Moxie Points column of the Pugilist Features table.
You can spend these points to enhance or fuel certain Pugilist features. You start
knowing three such features: Brace Up, One-Two Punch, and Stick and Move,
each of which is detailed below.
When you expend a Moxie Point, it is unavailable until you finish a Short or
Long Rest, at the end of which you regain all your expended points.
Brace Up. You can use a Bonus Action and expend 1 Moxie Point to brace for
attacks. When you do so, roll your Fisticuffs die, and gain a number of
Temporary Hit Points equal to the number rolled plus your Pugilist level and
your Constitution modifier. These Temporary Hit Points vanish if any remain
after 10 minutes.
One-Two Punch. You can expend 1 Moxie Point to make two Unarmed Strikes
as a Bonus Action.
Stick and Move. You can use a Bonus Action and expend 1 Moxie Point to make
an Unarmed Strike and take the Dash or Disengage action.

**흰 고릴라 투척병의 턴:** Round 2

**매그너스의 턴:** (크아악 내가 무기 사거리가 35피트인데
(하필 40피트야

**Reckless Attack:** You can throw aside all concern for defense to attack with increased ferocity.
When you make your first attack roll on your turn, you can decide to attack
recklessly. Doing so gives you Advantage on attack rolls using Strength until the
start of your next turn, but attack rolls against you have Advantage during that
time.

**이브:** 비알
용의 분노 지팡이 [Shillelagh]
이 무기로 공격 굴림에서 20이 나올 때마다, 대상으로부터 5피트 이내에 있는 선택한 각 생
명체는 5의 번개 피해를 입습니다.
행동으로, 무기에서 9미터(30피트) 반경의 파괴적인 에너지 원뿔을 방출할 수 있습니다. 해
당 범위 내의 모든 생명체는 민첩성 내성 굴림(난이도 16)을 해야 하며, 실패 시 8d6의 번개
피해를 입고, 성공 시에는 절반의 피해를 입습니다. 이 행동은 한 번 사용하면 다음 날 새벽까
지 다시 사용할 수 없습니다.
🎲 1d20 + 3 + max(-2,6) + 2 = 14

**Gamemaster:** 흰 팔 원숭이(도끼) takes 15 damage

**HP 업데이트 됨 두 배 적용 취소:** x1
27-15(15)=12

**이브:** 비알
용의 분노 지팡이 [Shillelagh]
이 무기로 공격 굴림에서 20이 나올 때마다, 대상으로부터 5피트 이내에 있는 선택한 각 생
명체는 5의 번개 피해를 입습니다.
행동으로, 무기에서 9미터(30피트) 반경의 파괴적인 에너지 원뿔을 방출할 수 있습니다. 해
당 범위 내의 모든 생명체는 민첩성 내성 굴림(난이도 16)을 해야 하며, 실패 시 8d6의 번개
피해를 입고, 성공 시에는 절반의 피해를 입습니다. 이 행동은 한 번 사용하면 다음 날 새벽까
지 다시 사용할 수 없습니다.
🎲 1d20 + 3 + max(-2,6) + 2 = 29
🎲 1d10 + max(-2,6) + 0 + 2 = 9
🎲 2d6 = 6

**Mugfist Knuckles:** These brass knuckles are plated with cheap faux gold that wouldn’t fool even
the most casual observer.
You gain a +1 bonus to attack rolls and damage rolls made with this magic
weapon. When you score a Critical Hit against an enemy with this magic
weapon, you gain GP equal to the creature’s Challenge Rating (or level if it does

🎲 1d8 + 5 + 1 = 13

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

A bright streak flashes from you to a point you choose within range and then
blossoms with a low roar into a fiery explosion. Each creature in a 20-foot-radius
Sphere centered on that point makes a Dexterity saving throw, taking 8d6 Fire
damage on a failed save or half as much damage on a successful one.
Flammable objects in the area that aren’t being worn or carried start burning.
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The damage increases by 1d6 for each spell slot
level above 3.

Cost: 2 Sorcery Points
When you cast a spell that has a casting time of an action, you can spend 2
Sorcery Points to change the casting time to a Bonus Action for this casting. You
can’t modify a spell in this way if you’ve already cast a level 1+ spell on the current
turn, nor can you cast a level 1+ spell on this turn after modifying a spell in this
way.

**Sorcerous Burst:** You cast sorcerous energy at one creature or object within range. Make a ranged
spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 damage of a type you
choose: Acid, Cold, Fire, Lightning, Poison, Psychic, or Thunder.
If you roll an 8 on a d8 for this spell, you can roll another d8, and add it to the
damage. When you cast this spell, the maximum number of these d8s you can add
to the spell’s damage equals your spellcasting ability modifier.
Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d8 when you reach levels 5 (2d8), 11
(3d8), and 17 (4d8).

**Cross Counter:** You can block the brunt of an attack and launch one of your own in the same
fluid motion. When you take damage from a melee attack, you can take a
Reaction and expend 1 Moxie Point to reduce the damage dealt to you by that
attack by 1d10 plus your Strength modifier and Pugilist level.
If you reduce the damage to 0, you can make an Unarmed Strike or attack with
a Pugilist weapon against a creature within your reach as part of the same
Reaction.

**안톤:** 마르도스

**Mugfist Knuckles:** These brass knuckles are plated with cheap faux gold that wouldn’t fool even
the most casual observer.
You gain a +1 bonus to attack rolls and damage rolls made with this magic
weapon. When you score a Critical Hit against an enemy with this magic
weapon, you gain GP equal to the creature’s Challenge Rating (or level if it does
not have a Challenge Rating). Creatures with a Challenge Rating less than 1
count as 0.
🎲 1d20 + 5 + 3 + 1 = 25
🎲 1d8 + 5 + 1 = 8

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**Moxie:** Your experiences of beating the odds have given you a moxie you can channel
in the midst of battle. This swagger is represented by a number of Moxie Points.
Your Pugilist level determines the maximum number of points you have, as
shown in the Moxie Points column of the Pugilist Features table.
You can spend these points to enhance or fuel certain Pugilist features. You start
knowing three such features: Brace Up, One-Two Punch, and Stick and Move,
each of which is detailed below.
When you expend a Moxie Point, it is unavailable until you finish a Short or
Long Rest, at the end of which you regain all your expended points.
Brace Up. You can use a Bonus Action and expend 1 Moxie Point to brace for
attacks. When you do so, roll your Fisticuffs die, and gain a number of
Temporary Hit Points equal to the number rolled plus your Pugilist level and
your Constitution modifier. These Temporary Hit Points vanish if any remain
after 10 minutes.
One-Two Punch. You can expend 1 Moxie Point to make two Unarmed Strikes
as a Bonus Action.
Stick and Move. You can use a Bonus Action and expend 1 Moxie Point to make
an Unarmed Strike and take the Dash or Disengage action.

**Reckless Attack:** You can throw aside all concern for defense to attack with increased ferocity.
When you make your first attack roll on your turn, you can decide to attack
recklessly. Doing so gives you Advantage on attack rolls using Strength until the
start of your next turn, but attack rolls against you have Advantage during that
time.

명체는 5의 번개 피해를 입습니다.
행동으로, 무기에서 9미터(30피트) 반경의 파괴적인 에너지 원뿔을 방출할 수 있습니다. 해

피해를 입고, 성공 시에는 절반의 피해를 입습니다. 이 행동은 한 번 사용하면 다음 날 새벽까
지 다시 사용할 수 없습니다.

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**Gamemaster:** 포션이 나왔을 때 샀어야지
네모(Nemo)

**순대:** Innate Sorcery
An event in your past left an indelible mark on you, infusing you with simmering
magic. As a Bonus Action, you can unleash that magic for 1 minute, during which
you gain the following benefits:
The spell save DC of your Sorcerer spells increases by 1.
You have Advantage on the attack rolls of Sorcerer spells you cast.
You can use this feature twice, and you regain all expended uses of it when you
finish a Long Rest.
네모(Nemo)의 턴

**순대:** 안톤

네모(Nemo)

**순대:** (그거 아마 발레리가 샀을걸요?

**그래서 못함:** Sorcerous Burst
You cast sorcerous energy at one creature or object within range. Make a ranged
spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 damage of a type you
choose: Acid, Cold, Fire, Lightning, Poison, Psychic, or Thunder.
If you roll an 8 on a d8 for this spell, you can roll another d8, and add it to the
damage. When you cast this spell, the maximum number of these d8s you can add
to the spell’s damage equals your spellcasting ability modifier.
Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d8 when you reach levels 5 (2d8), 11
(3d8), and 17 (4d8).

**밀메:** Positron Rifle
With a short phrase of void speech, you gather writhing darkness around your
hand. When you cast the spell, and as an action on subsequent turns, you can
unleash a bolt of darkness at a target within range. Make a ranged spell attack.
If your target is in dim light or darkness, you have advantage on the roll. On a
hit, the target takes 5d8 force damage and is frightened of you until the start of
your next turn.
At Higher Levels. When you cast the spell using a spell slot of 4th level or
higher, the damage increases by 1d8 for each slot level above 3rd.

**Fade Away:** You have learned to avoid notice at all costs, letting you momentarily obscure
yourself from observation. As a Bonus Action, you can take the Hide action to
conceal yourself without needing to be Heavily Obscured or behind Three-
Quarters Cover or Total Cover. You need not be out of a creature’s line of sight
to use this ability.
You become visible at the start of your next turn unless you have moved into a
position that allows you to use the Hide action normally. You can use this
feature a number of times equal to your Proficiency Bonus, regaining all
expended uses when you finish a Long Rest.

time.

Bloodied But Unbowed
When you take damage, you can take a Reaction to regain all your expended
Moxie Points. If you are Bloodied when you take this Reaction, you also gain
Temporary Hit Points equal to four times your Pugilist level. These Temporary
Hit Points vanish if any remain when you finish a Short Rest.
Once you use this feature, you can’t use it again until you finish a Short or Long
Rest.

**Mugfist Knuckles:** These brass knuckles are plated with cheap faux gold that wouldn’t fool even
the most casual observer.
You gain a +1 bonus to attack rolls and damage rolls made with this magic
weapon. When you score a Critical Hit against an enemy with this magic
weapon, you gain GP equal to the creature’s Challenge Rating (or level if it does
not have a Challenge Rating). Creatures with a Challenge Rating less than 1
count as 0.
🎲 1d20 + 5 + 3 + 1 = 22
🎲 1d8 + 5 + 1 = 10

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**Moxie:** Your experiences of beating the odds have given you a moxie you can channel
in the midst of battle. This swagger is represented by a number of Moxie Points.
Your Pugilist level determines the maximum number of points you have, as
shown in the Moxie Points column of the Pugilist Features table.
You can spend these points to enhance or fuel certain Pugilist features. You start
knowing three such features: Brace Up, One-Two Punch, and Stick and Move,
each of which is detailed below.
When you expend a Moxie Point, it is unavailable until you finish a Short or
Long Rest, at the end of which you regain all your expended points.
Brace Up. You can use a Bonus Action and expend 1 Moxie Point to brace for
attacks. When you do so, roll your Fisticuffs die, and gain a number of
Temporary Hit Points equal to the number rolled plus your Pugilist level and
your Constitution modifier. These Temporary Hit Points vanish if any remain
after 10 minutes.
One-Two Punch. You can expend 1 Moxie Point to make two Unarmed Strikes
as a Bonus Action.
Stick and Move. You can use a Bonus Action and expend 1 Moxie Point to make
an Unarmed Strike and take the Dash or Disengage action.

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**Mugfist Knuckles:** These brass knuckles are plated with cheap faux gold that wouldn’t fool even
the most casual observer.
You gain a +1 bonus to attack rolls and damage rolls made with this magic
weapon. When you score a Critical Hit against an enemy with this magic
weapon, you gain GP equal to the creature’s Challenge Rating (or level if it does
not have a Challenge Rating). Creatures with a Challenge Rating less than 1
count as 0.

**Moxie:** Your experiences of beating the odds have given you a moxie you can channel
in the midst of battle. This swagger is represented by a number of Moxie Points.
Your Pugilist level determines the maximum number of points you have, as
shown in the Moxie Points column of the Pugilist Features table.
You can spend these points to enhance or fuel certain Pugilist features. You start
knowing three such features: Brace Up, One-Two Punch, and Stick and Move,
each of which is detailed below.
When you expend a Moxie Point, it is unavailable until you finish a Short or
Long Rest, at the end of which you regain all your expended points.
Brace Up. You can use a Bonus Action and expend 1 Moxie Point to brace for
attacks. When you do so, roll your Fisticuffs die, and gain a number of
Temporary Hit Points equal to the number rolled plus your Pugilist level and
your Constitution modifier. These Temporary Hit Points vanish if any remain
after 10 minutes.
One-Two Punch. You can expend 1 Moxie Point to make two Unarmed Strikes
as a Bonus Action.
Stick and Move. You can use a Bonus Action and expend 1 Moxie Point to make
an Unarmed Strike and take the Dash or Disengage action.
네모(Nemo)

**마르도스:** 네모(Nemo)의 턴

gain a number of Temporary Hit Points equal to your Proficiency Bonus.
Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d6 when you reach levels 5 (2d6), 11
(3d6), and 17 (4d6).

**Font of Magic:** You can tap into the wellspring of magic within yourself. This wellspring is
represented by Sorcery Points, which allow you to create a variety of magical
effects.
You have 2 Sorcery Points, and you gain more as you reach higher levels, as shown
in the Sorcery Points column of the Sorcerer Features table. You can’t have more
Sorcery Points than the number shown in the table for your level. You regain all
expended Sorcery Points when you finish a Long Rest.
You can use your Sorcery Points to fuel the options below, along with other
features, such as Metamagic, that use those points.
Converting Spell Slots to Sorcery Points. You can expend a spell slot to gain a
number of Sorcery Points equal to the slot’s level (no action required).
Creating Spell Slots. As a Bonus Action, you can transform unexpended Sorcery
Points into one spell slot. The Creating Spell Slots table shows the cost of creating
a spell slot of a given level, and it lists the minimum Sorcerer level you must be to
create a slot. You can create a spell slot no higher than level 5.
Any spell slot you create with this feature vanishes when you finish a Long Rest.
Creating Spell Slots
Spell Slot Level Sorcery Point Cost Min. Sorcerer Level
1 2 2
2 3 3
3 5 5
4 6 7
5 7 9

**Positron Rifle:** With a short phrase of void speech, you gather writhing darkness around your
hand. When you cast the spell, and as an action on subsequent turns, you can
unleash a bolt of darkness at a target within range. Make a ranged spell attack.
If your target is in dim light or darkness, you have advantage on the roll. On a
hit, the target takes 5d8 force damage and is frightened of you until the start of
your next turn.
At Higher Levels. When you cast the spell using a spell slot of 4th level or
higher, the damage increases by 1d8 for each slot level above 3rd.

General Feat (Prerequisite: Level 4+)
You gain the following benefits.
Ability Score Increase. Increase your Strength or Dexterity score by 1, to a
maximum of 20.

throw, you can cause yourself to succeed instead. Once you use this benefit,
you can’t use it again until you finish a Short or Long Rest.

**Cross Counter:** You can block the brunt of an attack and launch one of your own in the same
fluid motion. When you take damage from a melee attack, you can take a
Reaction and expend 1 Moxie Point to reduce the damage dealt to you by that
attack by 1d10 plus your Strength modifier and Pugilist level.
If you reduce the damage to 0, you can make an Unarmed Strike or attack with
a Pugilist weapon against a creature within your reach as part of the same
Reaction.

**순대:** Sorcerous Burst
You cast sorcerous energy at one creature or object within range. Make a ranged
spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 damage of a type you

If you roll an 8 on a d8 for this spell, you can roll another d8, and add it to the
damage. When you cast this spell, the maximum number of these d8s you can add
to the spell’s damage equals your spellcasting ability modifier.
Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d8 when you reach levels 5 (2d8), 11
(3d8), and 17 (4d8).

time.

**Mugfist Knuckles:** These brass knuckles are plated with cheap faux gold that wouldn’t fool even
the most casual observer.
You gain a +1 bonus to attack rolls and damage rolls made with this magic
weapon. When you score a Critical Hit against an enemy with this magic
weapon, you gain GP equal to the creature’s Challenge Rating (or level if it does
not have a Challenge Rating). Creatures with a Challenge Rating less than 1
count as 0.
🎲 1d20 + 5 + 3 + 1 = 23
🎲 1d10 + 5 + 1 = 15

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**Speak with Plants:** You imbue plants in an immobile 30-foot Emanation with limited sentience and
animation, giving them the ability to communicate with you and follow your
simple commands. You can question plants about events in the spell’s area
within the past day, gaining information about creatures that have passed,
weather, and other circumstances.
You can also turn Difficult Terrain caused by plant growth (such as thickets and
undergrowth) into ordinary terrain that lasts for the duration. Or you can turn
ordinary terrain where plants are present into Difficult Terrain that lasts for the
duration.
The spell doesn’t enable plants to uproot themselves and move about, but they
can move their branches, tendrils, and stalks for you.
If a Plant creature is in the area, you can communicate with it as if you shared a
common language.

**Void Strike:** With a short phrase of void speech, you gather writhing darkness around your
hand. When you cast the spell, and as an action on subsequent turns, you can
unleash a bolt of darkness at a target within range. Make a ranged spell attack.
If your target is in dim light or darkness, you have advantage on the roll. On a
hit, the target takes 5d8 necrotic damage and is frightened of you until the start
of your next turn.
At Higher Levels. When you cast the spell using a spell slot of 4th level or
higher, the damage increases by 1d8 for each slot level above 3rd.

**매그너스:** (5d8 사령뎀이구나

**명중굴림이라는게 좋네:** 카이젤린

**밀메:** Positron Rifle
With a short phrase of void speech, you gather writhing darkness around your
hand. When you cast the spell, and as an action on subsequent turns, you can
unleash a bolt of darkness at a target within range. Make a ranged spell attack.
If your target is in dim light or darkness, you have advantage on the roll. On a
hit, the target takes 5d8 force damage and is frightened of you until the start of
your next turn.
At Higher Levels. When you cast the spell using a spell slot of 4th level or
higher, the damage increases by 1d8 for each slot level above 3rd.

**순대:** Font of Magic
You can tap into the wellspring of magic within yourself. This wellspring is
represented by Sorcery Points, which allow you to create a variety of magical
effects.
You have 2 Sorcery Points, and you gain more as you reach higher levels, as shown
in the Sorcery Points column of the Sorcerer Features table. You can’t have more
Sorcery Points than the number shown in the table for your level. You regain all
expended Sorcery Points when you finish a Long Rest.
You can use your Sorcery Points to fuel the options below, along with other
features, such as Metamagic, that use those points.
Converting Spell Slots to Sorcery Points. You can expend a spell slot to gain a
number of Sorcery Points equal to the slot’s level (no action required).
Creating Spell Slots. As a Bonus Action, you can transform unexpended Sorcery
Points into one spell slot. The Creating Spell Slots table shows the cost of creating
a spell slot of a given level, and it lists the minimum Sorcerer level you must be to
create a slot. You can create a spell slot no higher than level 5.
Any spell slot you create with this feature vanishes when you finish a Long Rest.
Creating Spell Slots
Spell Slot Level Sorcery Point Cost Min. Sorcerer Level
1 2 2
2 3 3
3 5 5
4 6 7
5 7 9

**Fireball:** A bright streak flashes from you to a point you choose within range and then
blossoms with a low roar into a fiery explosion. Each creature in a 20-foot-
radius Sphere centered on that point makes a Dexterity saving throw, taking
8d6 Fire damage on a failed save or half as much damage on a successful one.
Flammable objects in the area that aren’t being worn or carried start burning.
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The damage increases by 1d6 for each spell
slot level above 3.

8d6 Force damage on a failed save or half as much damage on a successful one.

slot level above 3.

**매그너스:** Rage
You can imbue yourself with a primal power called Rage, a force that grants you
extraordinary might and resilience. You can enter it as a Bonus Action if you
aren’t wearing Heavy armor.
You can enter your Rage the number of times shown for your Barbarian level in
the Rages column of the Barbarian Features table. You regain one expended use
when you finish a Short Rest, and you regain all expended uses when you finish a
Long Rest.
While active, your Rage follows the rules below.
Damage Resistance. You have Resistance to Bludgeoning, Piercing, and Slashing
damage.
Rage Damage. When you make an attack using Strength—with either a weapon
or an Unarmed Strike—and deal damage to the target, you gain a bonus to the
damage that increases as you gain levels as a Barbarian, as shown in the Rage
Damage column of the Barbarian Features table.
Strength Advantage. You have Advantage on Strength checks and Strength
saving throws.
No Concentration or Spells. You can’t maintain Concentration, and you can’t
cast spells.
Duration. The Rage lasts until the end of your next turn, and it ends early if you
don Heavy armor or have the Incapacitated condition. If your Rage is still active
on your next turn, you can extend the Rage for another round by doing one of
the following:
Make an attack roll against an enemy.
Force an enemy to make a saving throw.
Take a Bonus Action to extend your Rage.
Each time the Rage is extended, it lasts until the end of your next turn. You can
maintain a Rage for up to 10 minutes.

**이브:** 비알
지혜 내성 굴림12 🎲 1d20 + 6 + 3 = 12
Evolution/Devolution
By touching a creature, you can cause it to take on attributes of its ancestors or
descendants. A creature may accept these changes willingly or, if not, they must
make a Wisdom Saving Throw against your spell save DC. On a failed save, you
may pick one of the following changes and apply it to the creature’s stat block.
1 - Increase or decrease the damage of all of the creature’s attacks by 1d4.
2 - Increase or decrease the creature’s speed by 20 ft.
3 - The creature gains a climbing speed equal to half its speed, or its
climbing speed is reduced by 30 ft. (it can be reduced to 0).
4 - The creature gains a flying speed of 10 ft., or its flying speed is reduced
by 30 ft. (it can be reduced to 0).
5 - Select one of the creature’s attacks or abilities that deals damage and
change the damage type of that attack. If it deals Bludgeoning, Piercing, or
Slashing damage, you may change it to Acid or Poison damage. If it deals
any other damage type, you may change it to Bludgeoning, Piercing, or
Slashing damage.
6 - The creature gains Darkvision 60 ft., or reduces its Darkvision (if it has it)
by 60 ft. (it can be reduced to 0). If this creature does not have Darkvision,
you may alternatively reduce its maximum normal vision range to 60 ft.
instead, causing anything beyond 60 ft. from it to only be visible as
amorphous blurry shapes.
7 - Increase the creature’s maximum and current hit points by 1d4 + 4, or
reduce its maximum and current hit points by 1d4 + 4 (to a minimum of 1).
At Higher Levels: When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 3rd level or
higher, you may pick another Trait to change for each slot above 2nd level. You
cannot pick the same Trait more than once.

Advantage on Death Saving Throws, and once per turn, when a creature within 5
feet of the target hits it with a melee attack roll, the attacker takes 2d4 Necrotic
damage.

**Cross Counter:** You can block the brunt of an attack and launch one of your own in the same
fluid motion. When you take damage from a melee attack, you can take a
Reaction and expend 1 Moxie Point to reduce the damage dealt to you by that
attack by 1d10 plus your Strength modifier and Pugilist level.
If you reduce the damage to 0, you can make an Unarmed Strike or attack with
a Pugilist weapon against a creature within your reach as part of the same
Reaction.
🎲 (1d10 + 5) + 5 = 20

weapon. When you score a Critical Hit against an enemy with this magic
weapon, you gain GP equal to the creature’s Challenge Rating (or level if it does

count as 0.

흰 팔 원숭이(도끼)

**Gamemaster:** 근력 내성 굴림27 🎲 1d20 + 5 + 2 = 27

**안톤:** 마르도스

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**안톤:** 마르도스

**Moxie:** Your experiences of beating the odds have given you a moxie you can channel
in the midst of battle. This swagger is represented by a number of Moxie Points.
Your Pugilist level determines the maximum number of points you have, as
shown in the Moxie Points column of the Pugilist Features table.
You can spend these points to enhance or fuel certain Pugilist features. You start
knowing three such features: Brace Up, One-Two Punch, and Stick and Move,
each of which is detailed below.
When you expend a Moxie Point, it is unavailable until you finish a Short or
Long Rest, at the end of which you regain all your expended points.
Brace Up. You can use a Bonus Action and expend 1 Moxie Point to brace for
attacks. When you do so, roll your Fisticuffs die, and gain a number of
Temporary Hit Points equal to the number rolled plus your Pugilist level and
your Constitution modifier. These Temporary Hit Points vanish if any remain
after 10 minutes.
One-Two Punch. You can expend 1 Moxie Point to make two Unarmed Strikes
as a Bonus Action.
Stick and Move. You can use a Bonus Action and expend 1 Moxie Point to make
an Unarmed Strike and take the Dash or Disengage action.

**Gamemaster:** 매그너스 takes 8 damage

**HP 업데이트 됨 두 배 적용 취소:** x1

**Shillelagh:** A Club or Quarterstaff you are holding is imbued with nature’s power. For the
duration, you can use your spellcasting ability instead of Strength for the attack
and damage rolls of melee attacks using that weapon, and the weapon’s
damage die becomes a d8. If the attack deals damage, it can be Force damage
or the weapon’s normal damage type (your choice).
The spell ends early if you cast it again or if you let go of the weapon.
Cantrip Upgrade. The damage die changes when you reach levels 5 (d10), 11
(d12), and 17 (2d6).

용의 분노 지팡이 [Shillelagh]
이 무기로 공격 굴림에서 20이 나올 때마다, 대상으로부터 5피트 이내에 있는 선택한 각 생
명체는 5의 번개 피해를 입습니다.
행동으로, 무기에서 9미터(30피트) 반경의 파괴적인 에너지 원뿔을 방출할 수 있습니다. 해
당 범위 내의 모든 생명체는 민첩성 내성 굴림(난이도 16)을 해야 하며, 실패 시 8d6의 번개
피해를 입고, 성공 시에는 절반의 피해를 입습니다. 이 행동은 한 번 사용하면 다음 날 새벽까
지 다시 사용할 수 없습니다.
🎲 2d20kh + 3 + max(-2,6) + 2 = 16
🎲 1d10 + max(-2,6) + 1d4 + 0 + 2 = 17

네모(Nemo)

**순대:** (우선 크리터지면 저스티스 써드림
네모(Nemo)의 턴

**순대:** Mirror Image
Three illusory duplicates of yourself appear in your space. Until the spell ends, the
duplicates move with you and mimic your actions, shifting position so it’s
impossible to track which image is real.
Each time a creature hits you with an attack roll during the spell’s duration, roll a
d6 for each of your remaining duplicates. If any of the d6s rolls a 3 or higher, one
of the duplicates is hit instead of you, and the duplicate is destroyed. The
duplicates otherwise ignore all other damage and effects. The spell ends when all
three duplicates are destroyed.
A creature is unaffected by this spell if it has the Blinded condition, Blindsight, or
Truesight.
"일렁이는 빛과 그림자의 경계를 비틀어 진실을 기만하니,
거울 너머의 허상들이 깨어나 나의 걸음을 따라 함께 춤추게 하라.
어리석은 적들의 시선을 빼앗고 예리한 칼날을 조롱하며,
실체 없는 잔상들 속에서 길을 잃고 헛된 허공만을 베게 만들어라."
Metamagic: Quickened Spell
Cost: 2 Sorcery Points
When you cast a spell that has a casting time of an action, you can spend 2
Sorcery Points to change the casting time to a Bonus Action for this casting. You
can’t modify a spell in this way if you’ve already cast a level 1+ spell on the current
turn, nor can you cast a level 1+ spell on this turn after modifying a spell in this
way.
매타매직 사용 및 페이와일드 샤드 아이템 효과로 와일드 매직 서지 굴림

**안톤:** 마르도스

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for

chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**Cross Counter:** You can block the brunt of an attack and launch one of your own in the same
fluid motion. When you take damage from a melee attack, you can take a
Reaction and expend 1 Moxie Point to reduce the damage dealt to you by that
attack by 1d10 plus your Strength modifier and Pugilist level.
If you reduce the damage to 0, you can make an Unarmed Strike or attack with
a Pugilist weapon against a creature within your reach as part of the same
Reaction.
🎲 (1d10 + 5) + 5 = 17

**Moxie:** Your experiences of beating the odds have given you a moxie you can channel
in the midst of battle. This swagger is represented by a number of Moxie Points.
Your Pugilist level determines the maximum number of points you have, as
shown in the Moxie Points column of the Pugilist Features table.
You can spend these points to enhance or fuel certain Pugilist features. You start
knowing three such features: Brace Up, One-Two Punch, and Stick and Move,
each of which is detailed below.
When you expend a Moxie Point, it is unavailable until you finish a Short or
Long Rest, at the end of which you regain all your expended points.
Brace Up. You can use a Bonus Action and expend 1 Moxie Point to brace for
attacks. When you do so, roll your Fisticuffs die, and gain a number of
Temporary Hit Points equal to the number rolled plus your Pugilist level and
your Constitution modifier. These Temporary Hit Points vanish if any remain
after 10 minutes.
One-Two Punch. You can expend 1 Moxie Point to make two Unarmed Strikes
as a Bonus Action.
Stick and Move. You can use a Bonus Action and expend 1 Moxie Point to make
an Unarmed Strike and take the Dash or Disengage action.

로부터 60피트 이내에 있는 생명체가 이점 또는 불이익을 적용하여 d20 주사위를 굴리려고 할 때
마다, 당신은 반응 행동을 사용하여 해당 주사위 굴림이 이점 또는 불이익의 영향을 받지 않도록 할
수 있습니다.

**비알:** 용의 분노 지팡이 [Shillelagh]
이 무기로 공격 굴림에서 20이 나올 때마다, 대상으로부터 5피트 이내에 있는 선택한 각 생
명체는 5의 번개 피해를 입습니다.
행동으로, 무기에서 9미터(30피트) 반경의 파괴적인 에너지 원뿔을 방출할 수 있습니다. 해
당 범위 내의 모든 생명체는 민첩성 내성 굴림(난이도 16)을 해야 하며, 실패 시 8d6의 번개
피해를 입고, 성공 시에는 절반의 피해를 입습니다. 이 행동은 한 번 사용하면 다음 날 새벽까
지 다시 사용할 수 없습니다.
🎲 1d20 + 3 + max(-2,6) + 2 = 13

**이브:** 비알
용의 분노 지팡이 [Shillelagh]
이 무기로 공격 굴림에서 20이 나올 때마다, 대상으로부터 5피트 이내에 있는 선택한 각 생
명체는 5의 번개 피해를 입습니다.
행동으로, 무기에서 9미터(30피트) 반경의 파괴적인 에너지 원뿔을 방출할 수 있습니다. 해
당 범위 내의 모든 생명체는 민첩성 내성 굴림(난이도 16)을 해야 하며, 실패 시 8d6의 번개
피해를 입고, 성공 시에는 절반의 피해를 입습니다. 이 행동은 한 번 사용하면 다음 날 새벽까
지 다시 사용할 수 없습니다.
🎲 1d20 + 3 + max(-2,6) + 2 = 28
🎲 1d10 + max(-2,6) + 1d4 + 0 + 2 + 1d6 = 22
🎲 2d6 = 2

**영체화:** 당신의 존재감이 변형되고 사라져 적들이 당신에게 해를 가할 수 있는 능력이 약해집니다. 1
분 동안 모든 적은 당신을 공격할때 불리점을 받습니다. 다른 사람의 공간을 통과할 수 있습
니다. 긴휴식당 숙련도 보너스만큼 사용할 수 있습니다.

적용하여 d20 주사위를 굴리려고 할 때마다, 당신은 반응 행동을 사용하여 해당 주사위 굴림이
이점 또는 불이익의 영향을 받지 않도록 할 수 있습니다.

**순대:** 동상이몽이었네
Metamagic: Careful Spell
Cost: 1 Sorcery Point
When you cast a spell that forces other creatures to make a saving throw, you can
protect some of those creatures from the spell’s full force. To do so, spend 1
Sorcery Point and choose a number of those creatures up to your Charisma
modifier (minimum of one creature). A chosen creature automatically succeeds on
its saving throw against the spell, and it takes no damage if it would normally take
half damage on a successful save.
"맹렬하게 휘몰아치는 마력의 폭풍 속에서도 온전한 통제를 잃지 않으니,
무자비한 파괴의 흐름을 정밀하게 비틀어 동료들이 머무는 곳에 안전한 피난처를 빚어내고,
재앙의 손길은 오직 우리의 적들만을 가려내어 자비 없이 휩쓸어라."

damage on a failed save or half as much damage on a successful one.

level above 3.

An event in your past left an indelible mark on you, infusing you with simmering
magic. As a Bonus Action, you can unleash that magic for 1 minute, during which
you gain the following benefits:
The spell save DC of your Sorcerer spells increases by 1.
You have Advantage on the attack rolls of Sorcerer spells you cast.
You can use this feature twice, and you regain all expended uses of it when you
finish a Long Rest.

**순대:** Justice 발동!
당신은 잠시 운명의 저울추를 맞출 수 있는 능력을 얻습니다. 앞으로 8시간 동안, 당신 또는 당신으
로부터 60피트 이내에 있는 생명체가 이점 또는 불이익을 적용하여 d20 주사위를 굴리려고 할 때
마다, 당신은 반응 행동을 사용하여 해당 주사위 굴림이 이점 또는 불이익의 영향을 받지 않도록 할
수 있습니다.

**아군의 불리점은 제거:** 하얀 바람 부족장 고룬노바 takes 12 damage

흰 팔 원숭이(도끼)

**Gamemaster:** Greataxe
Melee Weapon Attack:+7 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. Hit: 11 (1d12 + 5) 참격
damage.
🎲 2d20kh + 5 + 2 = 27
🎲 2d12 + 5 = 24

**안톤:** 마르도스

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**안톤:** 마르도스

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**이브:** 비알
용의 분노 지팡이 [Shillelagh]
이 무기로 공격 굴림에서 20이 나올 때마다, 대상으로부터 5피트 이내에 있는 선택한 각 생
명체는 5의 번개 피해를 입습니다.
행동으로, 무기에서 9미터(30피트) 반경의 파괴적인 에너지 원뿔을 방출할 수 있습니다. 해
당 범위 내의 모든 생명체는 민첩성 내성 굴림(난이도 16)을 해야 하며, 실패 시 8d6의 번개
피해를 입고, 성공 시에는 절반의 피해를 입습니다. 이 행동은 한 번 사용하면 다음 날 새벽까
지 다시 사용할 수 없습니다.
🎲 1d20 + 3 + max(-2,6) + 2 = 16
🎲 1d10 + max(-2,6) + 1d4 + 0 + 2 = 20

**🎲 2d6 =:** 안톤 takes 6 damage

**HP 업데이트 됨 두 배 적용 취소:** x1
36[16]-0[-6]=36[10]

**안톤:** 마르도스

**Cross Counter:** You can block the brunt of an attack and launch one of your own in the same
fluid motion. When you take damage from a melee attack, you can take a
Reaction and expend 1 Moxie Point to reduce the damage dealt to you by that
attack by 1d10 plus your Strength modifier and Pugilist level.
If you reduce the damage to 0, you can make an Unarmed Strike or attack with
a Pugilist weapon against a creature within your reach as part of the same
Reaction.

**매그너스:** Reckless Attack
You can throw aside all concern for defense to attack with increased ferocity.
When you make your first attack roll on your turn, you can decide to attack
recklessly. Doing so gives you Advantage on attack rolls using Strength until the
start of your next turn, but attack rolls against you have Advantage during that
time.

**흰 고릴라 투척병의 턴:** 안톤

**마르도스:** Moxie
Your experiences of beating the odds have given you a moxie you can channel
in the midst of battle. This swagger is represented by a number of Moxie Points.
Your Pugilist level determines the maximum number of points you have, as
shown in the Moxie Points column of the Pugilist Features table.
You can spend these points to enhance or fuel certain Pugilist features. You start
knowing three such features: Brace Up, One-Two Punch, and Stick and Move,
each of which is detailed below.
When you expend a Moxie Point, it is unavailable until you finish a Short or
Long Rest, at the end of which you regain all your expended points.
Brace Up. You can use a Bonus Action and expend 1 Moxie Point to brace for
attacks. When you do so, roll your Fisticuffs die, and gain a number of
Temporary Hit Points equal to the number rolled plus your Pugilist level and
your Constitution modifier. These Temporary Hit Points vanish if any remain
after 10 minutes.
One-Two Punch. You can expend 1 Moxie Point to make two Unarmed Strikes
as a Bonus Action.
Stick and Move. You can use a Bonus Action and expend 1 Moxie Point to make
an Unarmed Strike and take the Dash or Disengage action.

**매그너스:** "하나는 처리했어~"

**이브의 턴:** 비알

**Haste:** Choose a willing creature that you can see within range. Until the spell ends, the
target’s Speed is doubled, it gains a +2 bonus to Armor Class, it has Advantage
on Dexterity saving throws, and it gains an additional action on each of its turns.
That action can be used to take only the Attack (one attack only), Dash,
Disengage, Hide, or Utilize action.
When the spell ends, the target is Incapacitated and has a Speed of 0 until the
end of its next turn, as a wave of lethargy washes over it.
용의 분노 지팡이 [Shillelagh]
이 무기로 공격 굴림에서 20이 나올 때마다, 대상으로부터 5피트 이내에 있는 선택한 각 생
명체는 5의 번개 피해를 입습니다.
행동으로, 무기에서 9미터(30피트) 반경의 파괴적인 에너지 원뿔을 방출할 수 있습니다. 해
당 범위 내의 모든 생명체는 민첩성 내성 굴림(난이도 16)을 해야 하며, 실패 시 8d6의 번개
피해를 입고, 성공 시에는 절반의 피해를 입습니다. 이 행동은 한 번 사용하면 다음 날 새벽까
지 다시 사용할 수 없습니다.
🎲 1d20 + 3 + max(-2,6) + 2 = 15

**Sorcerous Burst:** You cast sorcerous energy at one creature or object within range. Make a ranged
spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 damage of a type you
choose: Acid, Cold, Fire, Lightning, Poison, Psychic, or Thunder.
If you roll an 8 on a d8 for this spell, you can roll another d8, and add it to the
damage. When you cast this spell, the maximum number of these d8s you can add
to the spell’s damage equals your spellcasting ability modifier.
Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d8 when you reach levels 5 (2d8), 11
(3d8), and 17 (4d8).

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.

its effect.

**매그너스의 턴:** 흰 팔 원숭이(투창)

**Gamemaster:** 몇몇 원숭이들은 모퉁이를 돌아서 옵니다.

**매그너스:** Reckless Attack
You can throw aside all concern for defense to attack with increased ferocity.
When you make your first attack roll on your turn, you can decide to attack
recklessly. Doing so gives you Advantage on attack rolls using Strength until the
start of your next turn, but attack rolls against you have Advantage during that
time.

**Gamemaster:** 흰 팔 원숭이(투창) takes 10 damage

**HP 업데이트 됨 두 배 적용 취소:** x1
28-10(21)=18

**매그너스:** Handaxe
Proficiency with a Handaxe allows you to add your proficiency bonus to the
attack roll for any attack you make with it.
🎲 2d20kh + 4 + 2 = 25
🎲 2d6 + 4 + 4 = 19
🎲 2 = 2

**이브:** 비알
용의 분노 지팡이 [Shillelagh]
이 무기로 공격 굴림에서 20이 나올 때마다, 대상으로부터 5피트 이내에 있는 선택한 각 생
명체는 5의 번개 피해를 입습니다.
행동으로, 무기에서 9미터(30피트) 반경의 파괴적인 에너지 원뿔을 방출할 수 있습니다. 해
당 범위 내의 모든 생명체는 민첩성 내성 굴림(난이도 16)을 해야 하며, 실패 시 8d6의 번개
피해를 입고, 성공 시에는 절반의 피해를 입습니다. 이 행동은 한 번 사용하면 다음 날 새벽까
지 다시 사용할 수 없습니다.
🎲 1d20 + 3 + max(-2,6) + 2 = 19
🎲 1d10 + max(-2,6) + 1d4 + 0 + 2 + 1d6 = 20

**🎲 2d6 =:** 흰 팔 원숭이(도끼) takes 20 damage

네모(Nemo)

**비알:** 네모(Nemo)의 턴

**순대:** Sorcerous Burst
You cast sorcerous energy at one creature or object within range. Make a ranged
spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 damage of a type you
choose: Acid, Cold, Fire, Lightning, Poison, Psychic, or Thunder.
If you roll an 8 on a d8 for this spell, you can roll another d8, and add it to the
damage. When you cast this spell, the maximum number of these d8s you can add
to the spell’s damage equals your spellcasting ability modifier.
Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d8 when you reach levels 5 (2d8), 11
(3d8), and 17 (4d8).
🎲 2d20kh + 3 + 3 = 23

**🎲 2d8x3=8 =:** 흰 팔 원숭이(투창) takes 9 damage

**HP 업데이트 됨 두 배 적용 취소:** x1
9-9(10)=0
네모(Nemo)

**순대:** Metamagic: Quickened Spell
Cost: 2 Sorcery Points
When you cast a spell that has a casting time of an action, you can spend 2
Sorcery Points to change the casting time to a Bonus Action for this casting. You
can’t modify a spell in this way if you’ve already cast a level 1+ spell on the current
turn, nor can you cast a level 1+ spell on this turn after modifying a spell in this
way.
매타매직 사용 및 페이와일드 샤드 아이템 효과로 와일드 매직 서지 굴림
/r 1d100
29 🎲 1d100 = 29
다음 1분 이내에 피해를 주는 주문을 시전할 때는 주문의 피해 주사위를 굴리지 마십시오. 대신 각
피해 주사위에서 나올 수 있는 가장 높은 숫자를 사용하십시오.
건강 내성 굴림10 🎲 1d20 + 4 + 3 + 1 = 10

**Gust Barrier:** You spread your arms wide, allowing yourself to become enveloped by the air
around you. Until the end of your next turn, any ranged attack against you is made
with disadvantage.
Melee attackers who successfully hit you must make a Constitution saving throw
against your spell save DC. On a failure, the attacker is flung away from you up to
10 feet and is knocked prone.

**하얀 바람 부족장 고룬노바의 턴:** Bless
You bless up to three creatures within range. Whenever a target makes an attack
roll or a saving throw before the spell ends, the target adds 1d4 to the attack
roll or save.
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. You can target one additional creature for
each spell slot level above 1.

**Mugfist Knuckles:** These brass knuckles are plated with cheap faux gold that wouldn’t fool even
the most casual observer.
You gain a +1 bonus to attack rolls and damage rolls made with this magic
weapon. When you score a Critical Hit against an enemy with this magic
weapon, you gain GP equal to the creature’s Challenge Rating (or level if it does
not have a Challenge Rating). Creatures with a Challenge Rating less than 1
count as 0.
🎲 1d20 + 5 + 3 + 1 + 1d4 = 21
🎲 1d10 + 5 + 1 = 12

You gain a +1 bonus to attack rolls and damage rolls made with this magic

흰 팔 원숭이(도끼)

**Gamemaster:** 흰 팔 원숭이(도끼)의 턴

**Gamemaster:** 안톤

**마르도스:** Unarmed Strike
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

time.

**순대:** Justice 발동!

로부터 60피트 이내에 있는 생명체가 이점 또는 불이익을 적용하여 d20 주사위를 굴리려고 할 때
마다, 당신은 반응 행동을 사용하여 해당 주사위 굴림이 이점 또는 불이익의 영향을 받지 않도록 할
수 있습니다.

명체는 5의 번개 피해를 입습니다.

네모(Nemo)

**순대:** 몸속 깊은 곳에서부터 통제할 수 없는 야생의 마력이 폭포수처럼 끓어오르며, 머리카락 끝과 양손
에서 짙은 푸른빛의 스파크가 사납게 튀어 오릅니다.
"오, 이런. 평소보다 마력이 조금… 아니, 아주 많이 과하게 솟구치는데 말입니다. 감당할 준비는
되었습니까?"
적을 향해 손을 뻗어 올리는 일순간, 자잘하게 얽히던 전류들이 단 한 치의 오차도 없는 완벽하고
거대한 뇌전으로 압축되며 대기를 찢어발길 듯 진동합니다.
"정말 운이 없었군요. 지금 제 손끝에서 터져 나갈 이 순수한 벼락에는, 단 1퍼센트의 자비도, 일말
의 불확실성도 섞여 있지 않습니다!"
고막을 찢는 파열음과 함께 쏘아진 눈부신 백색의 벼락은 주사위의 변수조차 허락하지 않는 절대적
인 파괴력으로 적을 단숨에 꿰뚫어 버립니다.
까맣게 타버린 대지 위로 짙은 오존 냄새가 진동하고, 아직도 공기 중에 찌릿찌릿하게 맴도는 압도
적인 야생 마력의 여운을 만끽하며 씨익 웃어 보입니다.

**Sorcerous Burst:** You cast sorcerous energy at one creature or object within range. Make a ranged
spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 damage of a type you
choose: Acid, Cold, Fire, Lightning, Poison, Psychic, or Thunder.
If you roll an 8 on a d8 for this spell, you can roll another d8, and add it to the
damage. When you cast this spell, the maximum number of these d8s you can add
to the spell’s damage equals your spellcasting ability modifier.
Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d8 when you reach levels 5 (2d8), 11
(3d8), and 17 (4d8).

You gain a +1 bonus to attack rolls and damage rolls made with this magic
weapon. When you score a Critical Hit against an enemy with this magic
weapon, you gain GP equal to the creature’s Challenge Rating (or level if it does
not have a Challenge Rating). Creatures with a Challenge Rating less than 1
count as 0.
🎲 1d20 + 5 + 3 + 1 = 19
🎲 1d10 + 5 + 1 = 11

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.
Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll
equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target
takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier.
Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw
and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency
Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger
than you and if you have a hand free to grab it.
Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it
chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

**Unarmed Strike:** Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick,
head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a
melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a
target within 5 feet of you.
Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for
its effect.

Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger

chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone
condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and
Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one
size larger than you.

weapon. When you score a Critical Hit against an enemy with this magic
weapon, you gain GP equal to the creature’s Challenge Rating (or level if it does
not have a Challenge Rating). Creatures with a Challenge Rating less than 1
count as 0.
🎲 2d20kh + 5 + 3 + 1 = 26
🎲 1d10 + 5 + 1 = 14
